[1;30r[27;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m# Make sure PORT transfer connections originate from port 20 (ftp-data).[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1Hconnect_from_port_20=YES[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m# If you want, you can arrange for uploaded anonymous files to be owned by[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m# a different user. Note! Using "root" for uploaded files is not[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m# recommended![39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m#chown_uploads=YES[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m#chown_username=whoever[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m# You may override where the log file goes if you like. The default is shown[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m# below.[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m#xferlog_file=/var/log/vsftpd.log[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m# If you want, you can have your log file in standard ftpd xferlog format.[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m# Note that the default log file location is /var/log/xferlog in this case.[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m#xferlog_std_format=YES[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m# You may change the default value for timing out an idle session.[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m#idle_session_timeout=600[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d

[1;30r[27;1H[36m# It is recommended that you define on your system a unique user which the[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d

[1;30r[27;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m# Enable this and the server will recognise asynchronous ABOR requests. Not[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m# recommended for security (the code is non-trivial). Not enabling it,[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d

[1;30r[27;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m# By default the server will pretend to allow ASCII mode but in fact ignore[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m# the request. Turn on the below options to have the server actually do ASCII[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m# mangling on files when in ASCII mode.[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m# Beware that on some FTP servers, ASCII support allows a denial of service[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m# attack (DoS) via the command "SIZE /big/file" in ASCII mode. vsftpd[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m# predicted this attack and has always been safe, reporting the size of the[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m# raw file.[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m# ASCII mangling is a horrible feature of the protocol.[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m#ascii_upload_enable=YES[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m#ascii_download_enable=YES[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m# You may fully customise the login banner string:[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d

[1;30r[27;1H[36m# You may specify a file of disallowed anonymous e-mail addresses. Apparently[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d

[1;30r[27;1H[36m# You may restrict local users to their home directories.  See the FAQ for[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d

[1;30r[27;1H[36m# You may specify an explicit list of local users to chroot() to their home[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d

[1;30r[27;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m# You may activate the "-R" option to the builtin ls. This is disabled by[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d

[1;30r[27;1H[36m# By default the server will pretend to allow ASCII mode but in fact ignore[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
[1;30r[27;1H[36m# the request. Turn on the below options to have the server actually do ASCII[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d

[1;30r[27;1H[36m# predicted this attack and has always been safe, reporting the size of the[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;28r8[28d
